I've been a Tenacious D fan since I saw the HBO special way back in the day. I saw them live during the Rize of the Fenix Tour, own every single album, and everything else they've released over the years. I've heard every song they've ever made, covered, etc. I have "The Complete Masterworks" (Vol. 1 & 2) on DVD, saw The Pick of Destiny on opening night... My point is I'm a HARDCORE D fan, have been since the beginning, so I've been well aware of how Incredible Jack's vocal abilities are for 20+ years now, and it still amazes me to this day. I'd kill to be able to sing like that. I feel like they're so underrated as an actual band, and looked at as a "joke band" by the people who don't actually listen to their music.
